## LeaderboardCompressedV3

  Returns the leaderboard for a tournament where payload contains the leaderboard data in Base64 encoding.

### Fields

| Field | Type | Description |
|-------|------|-------------|
| `id` | `ID!` |   The tournament ID |
| `payload` | `String!` |   The full leaderboard payload/response. Will need to be Base64 decoded by clients |
